Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	The cautery doesn't work for dropsy, except in the way that is called "asclepiades".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat according to the methods that we have described in sections, and your treatment is not beneficial, then it is necessary for you to make four cauterizations around the anus, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one under the breasts, and one behind the back on the spine, and one place on the buttocks; and let the cauterizations be very close to the spinal cord near the thigh.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les .ij. ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After allow the cautery to remain in place for a long time to burn off pus, and do not stop cleaning after the cautery; and healing would hasten, and the two intentions would come together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the belly is like the fork that we have demonstrated before; and for the back it's olive-shaped, according to what was placed here previously.
de l’enfleure des piez	regarding the swelling of joints
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the hands swell for someone who is hydroptic and filled with yellow bile, it's necessary that you apply the cautery between the thumb and the index finger on the back of the hand; and move your hand with the cautery without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And don't enter too far in the center, otherwise it would go beyond the yellow bile, and apply the cautery according to this shape:
Aprés fai sus .ij. jambes .ij. cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After performing on both legs, two cauteries each on the point of the cutticle in every leg; and have the cautery long, one near the knee before and the other behind, centrally in the leg; then leave the cauteries for a long time without treatment until something comes out; after curing other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	from memory
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai .i. grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et .iiij. cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout .i. cautere clavile subtil, et .ij. cauteres sus les hainches.	When the belly ache comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retaining and digesting power, which is in the stomach and within the intestines, is being overloaded and cannot be cured by regular treatments; you see that patient suffering a lot with very green symptoms, then make one major cautery on the stomach following how it was described previously or abdominal cautery, at the circulating cautery. And four minor cauteries inside the mouth in all places, making one major thin cautery for each point and two minor cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the body suffering, make a cautery on the bellybutton, and one cautery on each armpit, and two small cauteries in the stomach beneath the navel, because treatment benefits when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	regarding the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When there are hematomas or one or more at the base, and they are old, filled with large cold and moist corrupt humors, and if they have been treated as we've said in divisions without benefit, then apply a cautery: three on the spine of the back, that is completely beyond the center line between the ribs and belly button, gradually moving diagonally, and one cautery below the navel; and if you think the stomach has cooled down and the food isn't being digested, and you see swelling in the abdomen, then apply a large cautery on the stomach, as was mentioned before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with every part of the cautery. Leave the cautery for an extended period.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment until the wound heals.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Regarding the diseased area which is called "thehlul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble .i. raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou .ij., et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat the "thehlul" condition, if it appears as a rough area, and you apply the fire cautery that seems like a razor's edge, then set it fully ablaze over that "thehlul" treated spot; and keep your hand there until the flame reaches the base of the vein from which the blood flows; perform this once or twice, and if there is more "thehlul", cauterize each part as we have said; after the treatment with antiseptic ointments when they are effective; and if you cauterize with a large fire cautery over "alchatim", it will provide greater relief.
de plaie mal curee	Of improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear surgery or incision, as we will describe in its proper place, if such sickness occurs that can only be cured through cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	If there is no fistula and it has developed into putrefaction and corrupted moisture, if you need to try with a total test tool, and remember that you must know the size of the tool compared to the opening.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After shaving the cautery to resemble a rasp, and apply it to the fistula according to how much the tool has entered, and repeat the application of the cautery until the putrid and corrupted parts are burned away, once or twice or three times depending on your needs; and be careful not to burn nerves or large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula extends to the bladder and intestine, be aware of these symptoms, and do not perform this outside the body. Do it only during surgery and think that they are not passing away. After treating the wound until it heals, and if there is a discharge and the substances have lasted long, then you know the disease has been completely healed; and if the substances have not lasted, you will know that the disease remains and the bone is corroded at its root; and like one of these things we will mention in their body.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra .iij. cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When the pain in the stomach comes from the kidneys and large congestion, it affects women differently, hence you should apply a cautery on both sides of the kidneys with the same cautery we mentioned before; and if we cauterize at the midpoint, there will be three cauterizations in line, and they will provide more assistance.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et .i. a destre et .i. a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais .i. cautere defuers le dos, ou .ij. se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is full and weak due to heat and moisture so that the patient retains urine, then the practitioner should perform a cautery procedure on the lower part of the bladder, where hair begins near the thumb. On both right and left sides, each cautery should be as long as the span of one's hand; and apply a single cautery behind the back, or two if needed; and make sure the cauteries are in the shape described beforehand.
de la marris	Of the liver
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice .iij. cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et .ij. cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the liver is cold and moist, and fails to allow conception to occur, and the flowers (likely referring to some medical condition or symptoms) are putrefied with their ends delayed; and when they come in, there is much pain: then it's necessary to perform three cauterizations inside the womb, just as we have said about the cautery for the bladder, and two cauterizations behind the back; and make sure the cauterizations are made in the shape of a claw, as we have said.
de la hainche	From the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a .i. cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous fluids descend to the crotch area of the thigh, and because of this reason it moves out of its place. The signs are that the leg is longer than the other when measured together; and the limbs are found from the division visible point, then you should cauterize the diseased part on the crotch area of the thigh with one fire cautery resembling a circle, and mark before the limb inside the crotch so that the crotch be within the circle; and let the cauteries be as those used for cauterizing the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai .iij. cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you do not have these fire cauteries ready, make three olive-sized fire cauteries instead, and ensure that the cauteries are as large as all your nails; and treat with them until they cool down.
de la dolor de la hainche	Regarding the pain in the thigh
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the thigh bone, and this is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is treated using what we have discussed about treatment for joint disorders, but the cure does not work, and the disease is old: thus, it is necessary that you cleanse the body of its large fluids with putrid pills or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After performing the cautery; and the method of the cautery is according to two methods: this means combining hot medications, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery can follow many methods, among which one is like this: you apply three triangular cauterizations according to this shape on the buttock, making sure they have good depth and size, leaving space the width of two between each cautery, use olive oil as the cautery. No middle cautery is made in the center of the buttock, since there are four according to this shape:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that it is cauterized with the circular cautery as we have explained before in the dislocation of the thigh bone; but make it like this so that the circles contain all the thigh bone, and all the points around the wound are heated.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This is the method used for sciatica, when the pain stays in the buttock and does not reach up to the thigh or down to the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it reaches up to the thigh and leg, make two fires at this point or where the patient says it hurts, and make one above the ankle four times, a bit on the left side; then let these be cutler's fires, and burn off any thickening in the blood clot; and if the patient senses that the pain extends up to knee or close to it, cauterize here where he feels the pain three points or four at the fire point called 'points'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if more work is required, do it; and should the pain extend from the knee towards the thigh, use cutaneous or circular cauterization, and take great care in all your cauterizations to not let off until you burn both nerves and major arteries, and make no greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen several who had made a cautery on the ankle towards the knee, and they left it until the leg was completely swollen, and even the feet as well, causing all of them to become inflamed and rotten.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach ailment from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are together in two parts, make a cautery on each one, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the sage said about the cautery of the buttocks, as follows, make it a piece of metal the size of a small bird's claw or slightly smaller, and have it with crosspieces and these crosspieces should span from one to the other across an area equivalent in size to a small rope. And let the crosspieces be divided into two parts, and they should resemble knots, and ensure that the metal part is well made; this is its shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois .i. cautere reont et lou laisse .iij. jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it becomes entirely toasty red and you smell scents emanating from it, and then place it on the sore area of the hip wound, and rotate it over the healthy side. And apply this cautery once with one piece of iron, leave it for three days; and afterwards cover it in butter, and let the wound remain open long enough; after the ointment treatment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use a little of this cautery for the fear caused by its application, and we see few who use it; however, all the same, this is good cautery which one can endure, and allows where it happens.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cauterizing instruments of medicine are such that you make an instrument with crosspieces in which the edge descends into the opening, and it should be made of steel or long iron, and at its height it has two knots, and between each one is the size of a doig; they are open at both ends and above, and they join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing on the buttock of the lying patient with a clean costium, and quickly place your hand mostly over the buttock; afterwards put between the second circles of the hot embers which are heated in the fire pot for one hour exactly, and allow the patient to endure the heat and burn from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it finds biting also like from fire; and when the biting has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the buttocks gently, and leave thus for three days, and apply butter until what is black from the charred remains is turned over; and let it be left for three days until putrefaction had spread; and this would be the last help after the treatment of ointments as long as he's healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread up to the thigh or even to the leg, you do it with the same instrument as you did for the buttock equally; and this is the way of hot treatment, and I have written it down or treated it about correcting medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take equal parts of salt and live charcoal, as much of one as of the other, grind them together and mix them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	So that it has a small notch so that the tip of a razor may be able to enter; and put it in that pot into another well sealed pot, and place salt and charcoal underneath gently until there are two spoonfuls above the powders until you have thoroughly mixed them with your hand; and leave it like this until all the moisture and scum or wax drain out of it then when it is sealed, take all that mixture, and pour it onto charcoal and onto salt in the same manner as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And then it will be plenty of water and applied in the form of various substances of medicine and as cauterizers for other limbs. For it accomplishes a similar task to fire, and it is used with other medicines when you properly cauterize the buttocks like turpentine, honey, anacardium, and charcoal mixed with soap, all these things combined together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us about a treatment that some men were treated with for the pain in their hip and sciatic vein, and the back leg, and he says that no other treatment was done, and they became well after this treatment took place. And when it had been done, as he instructs later here, they bathed themselves accordingly.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And they instruct in this manner: take some green and dry verdigris and grind it finely with a bit of fat. Apply the mixture to the hip, thigh, and leg where pain is felt, and bind it there. Leave it on for three hours and ensure that the patient does not feel any burning sensation due to the quantity used.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then let them take a bath until their body is slightly stirred up, and then have them lie down, and the pain will completely go away and they will recover.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicines' cauterizing, if this is after the removal of pus.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides states that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with the fat of a goat, if it helps much; and the cautery should be performed in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lanoline and mix it with old oil, then apply it to the depression located between the base of the thumb and the other one called the fossa.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After taking the fat of a dried goat and heating it until it becomes charcoal, put this on wool, then leave it until it stains. Repeat this process again, not stopping until you think by sense that it will reach to the hip, and the pain is relieved; this method of cauterization is called "goat's cauterizing".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by fall or from percussion or due to too much evacuation, or through indications of spread of cold matter, none of these appearances warrant cauterization. For it is the one who comes from the infusion of cold matter that deserves cautery.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne .v. cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai .iij. cauteres ou .iiij. au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary that after the body has been emptied of fetid pills or other indications, one performs this on the back where the pain occurs, three lines marked with a cross, and in each line according to the virtue and quantity the body can endure, more than .v. cauterizations; and do the cauterizations according to the cautery called "points"; and if you see fit, perform 3 or 4 cauterizations at the mid clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often befalls small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they feel tightness alone when they stand up and faint; and you find in the last spine at the back and upon us the appearance that comes to other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this [condition] and observe its cure, if you treat it with the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If one applies a heated cautery to each part of the spine, it becomes equal.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see fit, apply the heated cautery to around the spine along the line of the hot instrument for two or three lines, and have the points close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment until it is healthy according to what we have said, and be cautious not to apply the cautery in a state of excitement that is near nerve channels.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain in joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain in joints is due to moisture that spreads throughout each limb, and when pain comes from inside the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it's caused by cold and needs medicine to cure it, then it can be treated using cautery in this way: make the shape of the cautery inside the joint of the foot, and apply olive oil to the cautery according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need that you touch at the foot of the cheekbone, if you make it cauterized across the whole instrument saying 'point' when done.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains extend up to the knees and other joints, when this happens often, you should apply cauterization at each knee for three or four cauterizers from each part, across all olive oil; and if it is necessary for more, do so but don't remove your hand until as soon as the heat of the wound has been heated.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, then administer the cautery as we have described in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, then make incisions between the second and third lines on the wrist; and if there remains no pain in the elbows, then make incisions on each joint and at the hair of the hand; and if the pains come up to the wrists or shoulders, then cauterize each part, and give good care to the patient and take medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	And if you give him good care and purge phlegm, then he will recover with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the scrotum
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When rupture happens in anger, and the bowels descend into intestines it's new, so it must be that when you see him being cured, he does not consume anything that day; and he should use things that lighten his stomach, so that his innards descend from his stomach; after have him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to shave off his armpit hair until the intestines are repaired, then pull them with your fingers, and scrape over the rupture on the bone of the finger, and at every sign it should resemble half a circle above the chest; then warm up the cautery as described here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and sheds pus.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the boils at their root; and instruct his ministers to scrape his hand so that it doesn't turn back; and work well on the thighs for the patient, and place one piece of charcoal and one sergeant on the thighs, and another under his buttocks where you scrape his hands; then apply the cautery to the sign on your whole hand, and keep your other hand straight until you reach the bone; and if you don't touch it the first time, try again several times until you get to the bone; and be careful not to allow pus to escape when you apply the cautery; do not burn him; and so that the patient doesn't suffer or from other illnesses.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach up to the bone with the cautery, your treatments are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it must be that the cauteries for children are subtle according to their size, and for the big people too large according to their size; after three days cleanse the wound with the wax of the cautery until the scab is removed; then apply other ointments until they heal properly, and let the patient lie on his back for forty days so that the wound heals well; and it must be that its rest periods are long enough so that the boils do not burst when he wishes to go into chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wants to stand up, get him a well-made girdle and wear it for another forty days; and have good rest, work him little and guard against drinking and eating too much, and don't strain his voice too high; and when he follows this advice, he will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say about after the amputation procedure in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	regarding the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And when it comes to wounds in other abdomens and they are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then I will apply the cautery as necessary according to their size, and it should be for three parts of the blood; after treating them according to what we have said; and none of the old ones have said that one must cauterize at the cautery in three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the start of infection and draw a line across the width above the wound, and another below, and guide your hand along the entire length of the bistort (cautery tool).
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and produce more pus.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in no limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any member, through falling or being struck, and this pain lasts long periods, and medicine does not cure it, then it should be cauterized with the fire cautery called "point", and apply the cautery according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it responds to the first cautery, that's good; if not, reapply another cautery over this one, because these are so designed they should affect the member nearest where you've applied them, thus you must apply the cauteries until the patient has responded.
de meselerie	Of cautery with fire, command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The medicines should be assisted with great help once for each cautery, and similarly the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the cautery? Take care that this disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, without relapse or lingering. You doubt whether corruption might spread throughout the body; then perform two cauterizations on the head: I place the head at noon, and the other towards the forehead at the end of hair; and II over the two horns, and I behind near the neck; and allow your hand so that the cautery reaches up to the bone, until the scabs come out sufficiently so that the vapors of the excess fluids can escape. And cauterize in secret as what was done beforehand.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et .i. cautere en som lou neis, et .ij. cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et .vj. cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et .i. grant sus la crupie et .i. autre delez, et .ij. sus les .ij. espaules; et .ij. sus les coutes, et .ij. sus les tendrons dou pis, et .i. sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et .i. autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et .i. autre sus lou foie.	And if the meseil is everywhere spread out; and it becomes apparent that you should cauterize with these cauteries we have said about earlier: on the head, and one cauterization in the nose area, and two cauteries on the spine from neck to shoulder, and six on the spine of the back, and a large one under the chin and another at its center, and two on each shoulder blade; and two over the ribs, and two on the tendons of the feet, and one over each joint of hands and feet, and over the hollows of the hands; be careful not to burn any nerves that are behind the heel, do not burn them. And never make a cauterization above the bone under the nail, and another over the bone of stomach, and another over the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	Know that when I perform more cauterizations, I provide more aid, and it benefits the patient; know that patients do not feel pain during cauterization as healthy people do, because their bodies are already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in the ways of metal tools.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, wash the wound with flour mixed with honey and other treatments until it becomes clean.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation appears in any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it does not become clean, then you make cauterizations on the limb according to its size and the size of the limb; and for each cauterization, let it go slightly into the flesh of the wound; then treat it with ointments until it becomes clean.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And each time one makes a cauterization on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that paralyzes the limb, and thus it is removed; and all the while no one should interfere unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	Of cautery with fire, command the sick person to let their hairs grow long and even; and if they poke at their root, hold their eyes still so they don't move until they fully grow.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the illness referred to as 'albaras' matures and medicine does not help, then cauterize using a small fire cautery according to the quantity of hair on the area. Do this until the boil is removed and its color changes; then cleanse with flour mixed with lentils, rose oil, and plantain leaves, along with colostrum and almond milk from each ingredient in equal parts. Mix all together, wrap with a cloth, and apply to the affected area until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment for the sore by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When ulcer begins, and you see it start to stop, if you detect it early, sear it with the cautery that seems like a circle, all around the circumference of the ulcer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And nevertheless the wise say that one should also cauterize in the middle of the ulcer; and nevertheless I do not think this is good, for fear it might become septic and deteriorate, and I have already decided never to do so; and a more correct practice would be to cauterize around (the circumference), using the cautery that's called 'circular', as we mentioned earlier when discussing different types of cauterizing.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the swelling that cannot die away
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called 'adubelati', and it takes time to die due to excessive bleeding or the patient's old age when they are worn out (meaning they're very old) and have little blood, or because of their strength; and you see them dying slowly: then sear around using several small cauterizations. Afterwards, leave them as such.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced through completely by the cautery, so heat the cautery as shown below:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the midst of that disease called "adubelati" while the fire is piercing the skin, and make such actions with the fire that the patient feels it outwardly in this manner so that the progress of the infection may be relieved.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure as long as it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure by fire using iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is one called "corrodens", and it is nothing else than a member's ulceration, for it eats away at the members as if they were dry branches.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in them that can bear a mixture of fire cautery, then prepare the fire cauteries very small and large according to what is suitable for the body or where the illness is; after that cauterize all around as long as you rid it of all corruption, leaving nothing behind, ensuring that everything corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and apply heat to the affected limbs with oil as long as the blisters caused by the fire have healed over, and all infection.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of wounds that cause pus.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days you see that healthy pus does not appear, it's good; and if this doesn't happen, then reapply the cautery to where it was left on the infected limbs.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has been treated with medicine instead of the fire cautery at times; but nonetheless, the fire cautery is a greater help. I have already mentioned the treatment for fever medicine in its section: take it when you need to.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	From those who come to the stones
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Sometimes, when bones emerge from the skin, a disease occurs that is called "enclosure" according to our understanding, and it's a large pus-filled lump that irritates the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the medical practices for this disease are done through two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This means: It is to be known as fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	The fire cautery is that you heat one of the metal points like a feather from a goose until it's very hot, and make them out of good iron to a size that can hold onto nails in all directions, with delicate edges; after this, place the heated point on the nail completely all around until it reaches the end of the nail; then leave it like this for three days until the process starts to produce gangrene; afterwards, prepare an ointment from powdered salve and apply it overnight as a covering over everything. This allows the nail to fall out cleanly along with its root.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound by applying salve until it heals.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are removed through wounds from the chest, and it happens repeatedly in hands and feet, you should bring in a hot cautery for this. And do it as follows: take an arnica stick or iron rod, or a goose feather, place them on a nail and on your thumb, meaning for warts; then put the stick over so that its tip touches all around, then apply some hot water, hold well with your hand, press your hand back until the edge of the stick touches the base of the nail, and then find that the hot water penetrates deeply to the root; and let the patient endure a short burn from the hot water for an hour; then leave it like this, and all will be removed at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	So treat one after another, until you have healed all within the body, then cleanse of those that generate pus.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment for shaking
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices .iiij. cauteres ou .iv. sus l’espinee dou dos, .i. cautere entre chescune espinee; et .i. cautere ou pez, et .i. sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When some shake from cold or nerves, or from the quartan fever or other causes, it is fitting that you apply four or five cauterizations to the spine of the back. Apply one cautery between each vertebra; and one on the chest with an olive oil cautery; if this does not stop the shaking, hasten the recovery of the patient's health from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	The pus-sores
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	None of the times visible through the skin or pus-filled swellings, that come from large corrupted masses.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	When they become visible, it is necessary at the first stage that you apply a small cauterizing tool to each tip of the pustule: a fine stick from myrtle wood, whose point is taken with fire, or from the long root of aristolochia, or on the lens-shaped cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And none of the times they are cauterized at the beginning according to this manner, and they do not grow pus before, but it dispels the superfluities from which they come, and they are cured; but it must be done after blood has been evacuated.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there occur great streams of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound when it flows outwards, or during incisions on an abscess, or with the cautery applied to limbs, and similar situations; it is much distressing to hear this.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren .i., ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And yet, when this happens to anyone, if you need to quickly place your index finger on the vein wound and apply pressure until the pain subsides under your finger, and no more drops leak out; then heat various small and large olive oil lamps until they are all red. Then take one (or adjust based on the size of the wound and the location of the artery), and position it over the vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery in place as long as the pain is relieved.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cautery is off the fire, then quickly take another one (.i., meaning 'one') of the cauterizing tools that are on the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des .iiij. manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after another until the bone is broken; and be careful that you don't burn the nerve which lies beneath it, nor allow any harm to come upon the patient; and know that when the bone breaks from the artery, you may not properly set it by yourself even if the artery is large, unless done through one of four ways as we have said: by cautery, or extraction when it hasn't been treated yet, or with a strong hold on a thread, or through medicine placed upon it which has power to set blood; and then bind and restrain it immediately afterwards.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the setting of a fractured limb by tightly binding it with cloths or placing burning objects upon it, or other similar actions, if they do not benefit when done correctly.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any sight or medicine nearby, then they should place their thumb on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it well until the bone is set both over the wound and over the vein; and do not move the arm but keep it moist with cold water often until it becomes very cold, until the bone is frozen, swollen and set. And make incisions in front of what needs cautery or medicine treatment.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of treatments for amputations
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have explained in the first chapter all illnesses for which fire cautery or hot medicine is required, including the applications and causes, as well as the instruments and forms of cauterization. I ended that chapter at the knee joint, and now I will proceed through this chapter using the same approach because we find more easily what we want here.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And as I begin this one, it is necessary for you, dear reader, to understand that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first chapter of cauterizations, so more caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the course of this chapter, there are often instances of blood evacuation when opening veins and incising abscesses, as well as treatment for wounds, extraction of arrows, cutting into stones, and similar matters; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you not to engage in foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For few people come for treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	if they come from such individuals who barely recover even with their illness and die quickly due to the panic they find in their disease, and because of the severity of their suffering; and one must have fear for these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And about these individuals who give their meaning and say: "Wait, I'm scared"; and the disease is cruel.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not right that you consent to those who come to you in this manner, but place more respect for your honor than for your greed, and do not act recklessly but wisely towards those you are certain of and can take care; and use prediction and indication in the treatments of your sick people whose health is restored; and this will help you acquire good reputation, glory, and lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, our Lords grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have instructed you this chapter by chapters, according to what is before or the section on cauterization, that I have outlined from head to feet, for you find it more easily of what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	from the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this illness comes very often to children at birth, and when the mother presses too hard on the head of the child; and it also happens sometimes due to reasons unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I never see this illness occur except in children, and among all those I have seen, their death came quickly; and because of that, it seems to me that it would be better for me to abandon the task of treating such illnesses partially.
Et je vis .i. enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com .ij. nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw two infants of this condition, the shoulder was filled with water, and the head swelled each day until it couldn't bear it anymore; he believed in so much moisture that he died, and this moisture is assembled underneath the bone near the axilla, between the muscle and the bone. And the incisions are such that if there's moisture between the muscle and bone, and the abscesses are small, you cut through the head one wide slit; and it should be as long as two fingers, as long as the moisture flows; and see this form of the spathilium:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	And if there's more moisture, and the abscess is larger, make two cuts in a manner resembling a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief .iij. fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is underneath the bone, and you see that the edges of the head open from each part, and water splashes when you press it with your hand on the inside, and this does not respond to your touch: then you must make three cuts in the middle of the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture completely outwards.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After holding the cuts of the bandages and powders, then I put wine and oil, and let it remain like this until the fifth day; after that, remove them, treat the wound with dressings and ointments, and let the head heal evenly. Then allow the patient to eat dried meat from a source free of moisture as long as the limb is comfortable and restored.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is that you look at where the opening of the abscess lies, and align with the water; for it never stands before; never behind; neither to the right; nor to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Cut therefore where the abscess opens, and where water fills it, and cut in accordance with what you can do; and be careful not to touch an artery; and watch for a flow of blood, so that the patient dies due to the release of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of cautery treatment instructs to allow hair growth long and even; if they are sharp at their roots, hold tightly so they do not move until fully grown.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When any disease called 'catarrh' affects the eyes or anus, and it's an old ailment, and medical remedies don't help, then the last resort treatment is to use a cautery with cutting off of both arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, when you see them able to do so, let the patients take off their head covers; after that, rub their heads with a rough cloth until the veins are visible. Then remove their hair from all around up to the neck. Next, look where the pulse is taken and examine both sides of each ear after the hair has been removed there as well, ensuring the ears have fully recovered. Then mark the ears with charcoal, then shave both ears with a sharp knife until the flesh is exposed at the bone, doing this while considering the size of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it, block the spur off of the artery and vein above, by cutting as well as two inches through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is severed, make sure that the heart continues to pump blood upwards constantly outside.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery doesn't open upon feeling, it is necessary that you measure the size of the space to be three fingers wide. Then gently press and continue until you reach the bone; and what needs to come out for blood is six cubic centimeters, and by chance a little more or less depending on how the patient can tolerate it, as well as the filling of the artery. Then look at the wound: if there remains just at the edge of the bone pointy like the tip of a lance, if the pus from the abscess doesn't ascend, then press down and seal the wound, and apply ointment until it heals completely.
de emigrainne	Of the cautery treatment,
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old age comes and acute coughing occur, because of the moisture in tears and body heat around the temples and elsewhere for many years, it's a condition that can be treated with methods of medical cures and all this doesn't help. We extract veins from the temples and apply hot cauterization techniques as we have detailed.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	The method of extracting them is such that the patient feels on their temple's hairs, and you can hear the artery emerging from the temple, for it opens well with its pulsation, and responds only in some people who are too cold; and if it does respond, you guide the patient using a strip of cloth, then rub their head against a rough cloth, and heat it up with hot water until the artery clearly appears. Then take the silver cup that's shaped as follows:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then lightly scrape the skin until you feel the artery, then raise it using forceps and remove all the tissues that are beneath each part; and if the artery is thin, pierce it at the tip of the little finger, then clamp that section according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it isn't cut, then neither escapes all its pain completely.
Et trai dou sanc des .vj. c/, jusc’a .iij.; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en .ij. leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les .ij. liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And guide the blood from seven cuts up to three; and if the artery is large, it's necessary that you tie it with two threads of a strong silk line for seven lengths, so that putrefaction doesn't occur in front of the welding of the wound, nor repeatedly bleed; then cut off the excess between those two threads at that moment. And then, if you see fit, apply the cautery gently up to the bone as long as the joints are covered; and this is the rough work, if the patient doesn't have fever and has a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the cauterizations assist in finishing off moisture: for this is more assistance against moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de .ij. pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	When it comes to extracting arteries, one must fill the arm with old cotton and place well-made bandages on it; and when they are released, apply dry medicinal substances that produce pus and bandages until the wound heals. And if there's no artery bleeding, do your best with cautering tools or use the space filled with vitriol in your hand to ensure the wound is sealed; and if you don't have this on hand, place ice inside it until the bleeding stops, then rinse with cold water until the bleeding ceases, ensuring a proper seal. When the artery extracted is softer and lighter during extraction of the artery, you should cauterize the vein from that cautering tool cutting down two parts but ensure the cuts are well-spaced to preserve heat for longer periods.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the tools become too tight, they retain less heat.

des larmes	Of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure. Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And they named the old "wound healer", and when you treat someone with this illness, have them grow hair on their head or forehead, then make three cuts evenly across the forehead according to its length; and make one of the cuts halfway down the entire forehead in an upwards direction until it reaches the nose, and the other two cuts about twice as long at each side above the eyebrows, and be careful not to cut the arteries which are located above the eyebrows; keep your hand away from the continuation of the two lower jaws, and make each wound three inches wide across; have a piece of sponge and some cloths ready to wipe off any blood, then use a sharp tool from one side as shown here for treatment:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les .ij. fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.
